             addListener(document.forms[i], 'submit', decorate);
           }
         }
         for (var i=0; i <document.links.length; i++) {
           var href = document.links[i].getAttribute('href');
           if(href && href.indexOf('/checkout') >= 0) {
             addListener(document.links[i], 'click', decorate);
           }
         }
       });
     
 
     var originalDocumentWrite = document.write;
     document.write = customDocumentWrite;
     try { window.ShopifyAnalytics.merchantGoogleAnalytics.call(this); } catch(error) {};
     document.write = originalDocumentWrite;
 
     
         window.ShopifyAnalytics.lib.page(
           null,
           {"pageType":"home"}
         );
       
     
   });

       eventsListenerScript.async = true;
       eventsListenerScript.src = "//cdn.shopify.com/s/assets/shop_events_listener-f2c5800305098f0ebebdfa7d980c9abf56514c46d5305e97a7c476f7c9116163.js";
       document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(eventsListenerScript);

           <div class="thumbnail-overlay">
            <a class="hidden-product-link" href="/collections/freshwater-homepage/products/little-cleo" itemprop="url">
             Little Cleo
            </a>
            <div class="info">
             <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="acme-tackle,freshwater-homepage" data-details-text="View full details" data-formatted-price="$4.49" data-full-description='&lt;!--Start tab labels--&gt;
 &lt;ul class="tabs"&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;&lt;a class="active" href="#tab1"&gt;Description&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="#tab2"&gt;Spec Chart&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="#tab3"&gt;Video&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;/ul&gt;
 &lt;!--Start tab content--&gt;
 &lt;ul class="tabs-content"&gt;
 &lt;li class="active" id="tab1"&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;Second only to the news that salmon and steelhead were tearing up tackle in the Great Lakes was the discovery that Little Cleos were the surest way to catch them. To anglers in the know that wasn’t really news. &lt;br&gt;For over 30 years Little Cleos have been taking limit catches of gamefish throughout North America. The unique hump-backed shape of Little Cleo results in a seductive, wiggling action as the lure is drawn through the water. The illusion created is one of a fat baitfish, acting in an erratic, confused manner. This odd behavior triggers the predatory nature of the gamefish, who strike out of curiosity and anger, as well as hunger. This threeway appeal hooks them every time, and explains Little Cleo’s fantastic success — it’s famous countrywide as the one lure that takes all gamefish. &lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;li id="tab2"&gt;
 &lt;img src="//cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2113/5683/files/standardcleochart_large.png?v=1500256118" alt="" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;
 &lt;hr&gt;
 &lt;img src="//cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2113/5683/files/cleosize_large.png?v=1500256168" alt="" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1/16 oz. (2-4 lb. test) Fly rod, ultra-lite spinning Ideal for trout &amp;amp; panfish.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1/8-1/6 oz. (2-4 lb. test) Ultra-lite, light spinning &amp;amp; spincasting Ideal for trout, panfish, shad &amp;amp; smallmouth bass.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1/3 oz. (4-6 lb. test) Light spinning, spin casting Ideal for trout, smallmouth bass &amp;amp; pickerel.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1/4 oz. (4-6 lb. test) Light to medium spinning, spincasting &amp;amp; trolling Ideal for trout, bass, pickerel, landlocked salmon &amp;amp; walleye.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;2/5 oz. (8-12 lb. test) Medium to medium-heavy spinning, trolling &amp;amp; baitcasting in still or running water. Ideal for all larger fresh water gamefish.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;2/3 oz. (8-12 lb. test) Medium to medium-heavy spinning, trolling &amp;amp; baitcasting in swift or deep running water Ideal for all larger fresh water gamefish.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;3/4 oz. (10-14 lb. test) Medium-heavy spinning, trolling &amp;amp; baitcasting Ideal for big trout, salmon, steelhead &amp;amp; stripers.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1 1/4 oz. (10-14 lb. test) Heavy spinning, trolling &amp;amp; surface casting Ideal for stripers, lake trout, salmon, pike and muskies.&lt;/p&gt;

The illusion created is one of a fat baitfish, acting in an erratic, confused manner. This odd behavior triggers the predatory nature of the gamefish, who strike out of curiosity and anger, as well as hunger. This threeway appeal hooks them every time, and explains Little Cleo’s fantastic success — it’s famous countrywide as the one lure that takes all gamefish. \u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/li\u003e\n\u003cli id=\"tab2\"\u003e\n\u003cimg src=\"\/\/cdn.shopify.com\/s\/files\/1\/2113\/5683\/files\/standardcleochart_large.png?v=1500256118\" alt=\"\" style=\"display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cimg src=\"\/\/cdn.shopify.com\/s\/files\/1\/2113\/5683\/files\/cleosize_large.png?v=1500256168\" alt=\"\" style=\"display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e1\/16 oz. class=\"tabs-content\"\u003e\n\u003cli class=\"active\" id=\"tab1\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSecond only to the news that salmon and steelhead were tearing up tackle in the Great Lakes was the discovery that Little Cleos were the surest way to catch them. To anglers in the know that wasn’t really news. \u003cbr\u003eFor over 30 years Little Cleos have been taking limit catches of gamefish throughout North America. The unique hump-backed shape of Little Cleo results in a seductive, wiggling action as the lure is drawn through the water. The illusion created is one of a fat baitfish, acting in an erratic, confused manner. This odd behavior triggers the predatory nature of the gamefish, who strike out of curiosity and anger, as well as hunger. This threeway appeal hooks them every time, and explains Little Cleo’s fantastic success — it’s famous countrywide as the one lure that takes all gamefish. \u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/li\u003e\n\u003cli id=\"tab2\"\u003e\n\u003cimg src=\"\/\/cdn.shopify.com\/s\/files\/1\/2113\/5683\/files\/standardcleochart_large.png?v=1500256118\" alt=\"\" style=\"display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cimg src=\"\/\/cdn.shopify.com\/s\/files\/1\/2113\/5683\/files\/cleosize_large.png?v=1500256168\" alt=\"\" style=\"display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e1\/16 oz.             <div class="info">
             <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="acme-tackle,freshwater-homepage" data-details-text="View full details" data-formatted-price="$2.99" data-full-description='&lt;!--Start tab labels--&gt;

 &lt;/li&gt;

 &lt;img src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2113/5683/files/phoebechart.png?1792310258109146246" alt="" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;
 &lt;hr&gt;
 &lt;img src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2113/5683/files/diagram.png?98296749723116256276" alt="" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1/12 oz. (2-4 lb. test) for small trout, minnow-eating panfish like perch, crappie.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1/8 oz. (4lb. test) all around casting lure — for trout, panfish, pickerel – deadly as an ice fishing jig.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1/6 oz. (6 lb test) for trout, walleye, bass, pike, pickerel.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1/4 oz . (6-8 lb. test) for trout, walleye, bass, pike, pickerel, light salt water species.&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;1/2 oz. (8-12 lb. test) for steelhead, salmon, salt water species.&lt;/p&gt;

             <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="acme-tackle,freshwater-homepage" data-details-text="View full details" data-formatted-price="$9.99" data-full-description="&lt;h4 class=&quot;entry-title&quot; itemprop=&quot;name&quot;&gt;Hyper-Glide – Best Glide Bait for fishing.&lt;/h4&gt;
 &lt;!--Start tab labels--&gt;
 &lt;ul class=&quot;tabs&quot;&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;active&quot; href=&quot;#tab1&quot;&gt;Product Details&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;

 &lt;ul class=&quot;tabs-content&quot;&gt;
 &lt;li class=&quot;active&quot; id=&quot;tab1&quot;&gt;
 &lt;p align=&quot;LEFT&quot;&gt;The NEW Acme Hyper-Glide features an injected plastic minnow body with wings that resemble real fish fins and open each time the bait falls. As the wings open, the bait glides as if it's swimming. Fish it vertically in open water and ice fishing. Shake it vertically and the wings open and close quickly. Cast it in open water to cover an extreme area as you bring it back to the boat. The Hyper-Glide searches and hunts fish on every cast! Use this bait to catch every species of fish that swims. &lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;dir&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;• Life-like gill action from wings opening and closing&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;• Wings open and close creating a loud noise against the body&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;• Glides through the water&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;• Unprecedented jigging action&lt;/p&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;• VDrop System allows for vertical drop to get back on fish quickly&lt;/p&gt;

 &lt;div class=&quot;layoutArea&quot;&gt;
 &lt;div class=&quot;column&quot;&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;The Google Eye Jig is the combination of sight and sound &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;to trigger more bites in all water types! It’s Shockwave &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Rattle System has been designed to call fish in and trigger a bite. The Google Eye Jig can be rigged with your favorite Kalin's plastics, or with live baits, making it one of the most versatile fish catching lures in your tackle box. Cast it, Jig it, Twist it, Rip it, or use a slow steady retrieve along the bottom to match the mood of the fish. The high carbon steel Katana hook, colored in red, is precision sharpened, and hardened to ensure a piercing hookset. The life-like rattling jig head features a glass eye to reflect light and add additional visual dimension and action to the jig. Specially selected color patterns have been chosen to grab the fish's attention, and put more fish topside. Big fish don't stand a chance - The Google Eye Jig is sure to become the new standard by which all other jigs are measured. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

            <div class="info">
             <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="frontpage,freshwater-homepage,kalins" data-details-text="View full details" data-formatted-price="$4.49" data-full-description='&lt;!--Start tab labels--&gt;

 &lt;li class="active" id="tab1"&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;The Jerk Minnow features a slightly split tail that delivers a swift and lifelike action that minicks the swimming motion of common baitfish.  The baitfish profile that the Jerk Minnow offers, along with the spilt tail action will prove to attract almost every species of fish.  The versatile bait can be rigged in a diverse set of ways to give the fisherman multiple different options for fishing. 10 baits per pack.&lt;/p&gt;

            <span class="quick_shop ss-icon js-quick-shop-link" data-collection-handles="frontpage,freshwater-homepage,kalins" data-details-text="View full details" data-formatted-price="$4.49" data-full-description='&lt;!--Start tab labels--&gt;
 &lt;ul class="tabs-content"&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;&lt;a class="active" href="#tab1"&gt;Description&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="#tab3"&gt;Video&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;
 &lt;li class="active" id="tab1"&gt;
 &lt;p&gt;The Jerk Minnow features a slightly split tail that delivers a swift and lifelike action that minicks the swimming motion of common baitfish.  The baitfish profile that the Jerk Minnow offers, along with the spilt tail action will prove to attract almost every species of fish.  The versatile bait can be rigged in a diverse set of ways to give the fisherman multiple different options for fishing. 10 baits per pack.&lt;/p&gt;

        <h3 class="sub_title">
         <a href="/blogs/news/acme-spoons-for-hot-ocean-shore-action">
          ACME Spoons for Hot Ocean Shore Action
         </a>
        </h3>
        <p class="blog_meta">
        </p>
        <div class="excerpt">
         From the Gulf of Mexico off Texas all the way around to the Atlantic Ocean in the Northeast, our coastline offers a wide variety of inshore fishing opportunities. Whether it’s backcountry fishing in the bayous, casting to the mangrove roots, prowling the flats or working the rocky surfline, hard-fighting, great-eating fish are available to the light-tackle angler in sheltered waters close to home.
        </div>

        </a>

        <h3 class="sub_title">
         <a href="/blogs/news/sizmic-probably-the-best-soft-swimbaits">
          Sizmic – Probably The Best Soft Swimbaits
         </a>
        </h3>
        <p class="blog_meta">
        </p>
        <div class="excerpt">
         Talk to pro anglers about the most significant additions to tackle box and skill sets in recent years, and many will single out soft swimbaits.  Why? The swimbait is a “stealth” search bait in the hands of a skilled angler. It enables him to cover water quickly and find fish without setting off the “alarm” that baits with loud rattles, big vibration and extreme water displacement sometimes do.

   <script type="text/javascript">
    Currency.format = 'money_format';
   
 
   var shopCurrency = 'USD';
 
   /* Sometimes merchants change their shop currency, let's tell our JavaScript file */
   Currency.money_with_currency_format[shopCurrency] = "${{amount}} USD";
   Currency.money_format[shopCurrency] = "${{amount}}";
 
   /* Default currency */
   var defaultCurrency = 'USD' || shopCurrency;
   
   if ($(window).width() >= 768) {
     var $currencySelector = $(".top_bar .currencies");
   } else {
     var $currencySelector = $("#mobile_menu .currencies");
   }
   
   /* Cookie currency */
   var cookieCurrency = Currency.cookie.read();
 
   /* Fix for customer account pages */
   $('span.money span.money').each(function() {
     $(this).parents('span.money').removeClass('money');
   });
 
   /* Saving the current price */
   $('span.money').each(function() {
     $(this).attr('data-currency-USD', $(this).html());
   });
 
   // If there's no cookie.
   if (cookieCurrency == null) {
     if (shopCurrency !== defaultCurrency) {
       Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, defaultCurrency);
     }
     else {
       Currency.currentCurrency = defaultCurrency;
     }
   }
   // If the cookie value does not correspond to any value in the currency dropdown.
   else if ($currencySelector.length && $currencySelector.find('option[value=' + cookieCurrency + ']').length === 0) {
     Currency.currentCurrency = shopCurrency;
     Currency.cookie.write(shopCurrency);
   }
   else if (cookieCurrency === shopCurrency) {
     Currency.currentCurrency = shopCurrency;
   }
   else {
     Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, cookieCurrency);
   }
 
   $currencySelector.val(Currency.currentCurrency).change(function() {
     var newCurrency = $(this).val();
     Currency.convertAll(Currency.currentCurrency, newCurrency);
     jQuery('.selected-currency').text(Currency.currentCurrency);
   });
 
   var original_selectCallback = window.selectCallback;
   var selectCallback = function(variant, selector) {
     original_selectCallback(variant, selector);
     Currency.convertAll(shopCurrency, $currencySelector.val());
     jQuery('.selected-currency').text(Currency.currentCurrency);
   };
 
   function convertCurrencies() {
     if($currencySelector.val() && $currencySelector.val() != $currencySelector.data('default-shop-currency')) {
       Currency.convertAll($currencySelector.data('default-shop-currency'), $currencySelector.val());
       jQuery('.selected-currency').text(Currency.currentCurrency);
     }
   }
